  declare %_UI_keyswitch[16 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]

    %_UI_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] := %btn_activate[$i]
    %_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] := %mnu_keyswitch[$i]

    %_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13] := %btn_analyze[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $j := 0
  while($j <= (num_elements(%keyswitch_idx) - 1)) 
    if(%_UI_keyswitch[$j] # 0)
      %matrix_grid_x[$j] := (((9 * abs(sh_right(abs(1 + sh_right(abs($j) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))) + %matrix_grid_x[- (- ($j - 1) .and. sh_right(- ($j - 1), 31))]) + (get_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[- (- ($j - 1) .and. sh_right(- ($j - 1), 31))], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) * (1 + sh_right(abs($j) - 1, 31)))) + (6 * (1 + sh_right(abs($j) - 1, 31)))
    end if
    inc($j)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $j := 0
    while($j <= (num_elements(%keyswitch_idx) - 1)) 
      if(%_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $j] # 0)
        set_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $j], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, %matrix_grid_x[$j] + get_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $j], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
        set_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $j], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (18 + (25 * ($i + 1))) + get_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $j], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
      end if
      inc($j)
    end while
    inc($i)
  end while

  declare %randNoteValues[128]

  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%randNoteValues) - 1)) 
    $___M__Seed := (8088405 * $___M__Seed) + 1
    %randNoteValues[$i] := ((sh_right($___M__Seed, 8) .and. 16777215) mod 1000) + 1
    %randNoteValues[$i] := ($last_rand_value + %randNoteValues[$i]) mod 1001
    $last_rand_value := %randNoteValues[$i]
    %randNoteValues[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%randNoteValues[$i]) - 0.) * 1000.) / 1000.) + -500.)
    inc($i)
  end while

  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_rate__hold := ($sli_envRateHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_rate__sustain := ($sli_envRateSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_int__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_int__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_int__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_int__hold := ($sli_envIntHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_int__sustain := ($sli_envIntSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while

    while($i <= (num_elements(%keyswitch_idx) - 1)) 
      if(%_UI_keyswitch[($j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $i] # 0)
        set_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt8[get_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[$j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    inc($j)
  end while
  set_key_pressed_support(1)
  set_voice_limit($NI_VL_TMPRO_STANDARD, 128)
end on
function update__row_fonts
  $j := 0
  while($j <= 15) 
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%keyswitch_idx) - 1)) 
      if(%_UI_keyswitch[($j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $i] # 0)
        set_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[($j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt8[get_control_par(%_UI_keyswitch[$j * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    inc($j)
  end while
end function
function reset__keycolors
  %key[1] := 0
  while(%key[1] <= 127) 
    set_key_color(%key[1], $KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE)
    inc(%key[1])
  end while
end function
function c_update__keycolor_mapped0
  %key[1] := %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx30 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13]
  while(%key[1] <= %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx30 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14]) 
    set_key_color(%key[1], $KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE)
    if(%_keyswitch_mapped_notes[($keyswitch_idx30 * 128) + %key[1]] = 1)
      set_key_color(%key[1], $color00)
    end if
    inc(%key[1])
  end while
end function
function color_keyswitches
  %key[0] := 0
  while(%key[0] <= 15) 
    set_key_color(%keyswitches[%key[0]], $KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE)
    if((%_keyswitch[%key[0] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 1) and (%_keyswitch[(%key[0] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] # 127))
      set_key_color(%_keyswitch[(%key[0] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1], $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    end if
    inc(%key[0])
  end while
end function
function c_sustain_release0
  if($note_id10 # -1)
    note_off($note_id10)
    $release_id00 := play_note($release_note00, 50, 0, 0)
    set_event_par_arr($release_id00, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
    $dyn_release := 0
    while($dyn_release <= ($num_dynamic_layers40 - 1)) 
      set_event_par_arr($release_id00, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, (($dyn_release + $start_group10) + $num_dynamic_layers40) + $title_groups)
      inc($dyn_release)
    end while
    $note_id10 := -1
    $event_notes10 := -1
  end if
end function
function c_legato_release0
  if(($note_held = 0) and ($note_id50 # -1))
    $event_notes50 := -1
    $note_id50 := -1
    if($is_attack = 0)
      $release_id10 := play_note(get_event_par($note_id50, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE), 50, 0, 0)
      set_event_par_arr($release_id10, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
      %key[6] := 0
      while(%key[6] <= ($num_dynamic_layers60 - 1)) 
        set_event_par_arr($release_id10, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, ((((((((((%key[6] + $start_group40) + $num_rr40) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers60) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers60) + $title_groups) + ($num_dynamic_layers60 * $sustain_fx)) + $title_groups) + $trans_groups20) + $title_groups)
        inc(%key[6])
      end while
    end if
    $playpos := ((get_event_par($note_id50, $EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS) / 10) * (1 + (sh_right(140000 - (get_event_par($note_id50, $EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS) / 10), 31) .or. sh_right(get_event_par($note_id50, $EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS) / 10, 31)))) - (140000 * sh_right(140000 - (get_event_par($note_id50, $EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS) / 10), 31))
    fade_out($note_id50, real_to_int((((int_to_real($playpos) - 0.) * 229999.) / 140000.) + 1.), 1)
    change_vol($release_id10, - real_to_int((((int_to_real($playpos) - 0.) * -9500.) / 140000.) + 10000.), 0)
    get_event_ids(%active_ids)
    %key[6] := 0
    while(%key[6] <= (num_elements(%active_ids) - 1)) 
      if(not (($note_id50 = %active_ids[%key[6]]) or ($release_id10 = %active_ids[%key[6]])))
        fade_out(%active_ids[%key[6]], 250000, 1)
      end if
      inc(%key[6])
    end while
  end if
end function
function c_one_shot_release0
  $note_id30 := -1
  $event_notes30 := -1
end function
function update__keyswitch
  call reset__keycolors
  %key[2] := 0
  while(%key[2] <= 15) 
    set_key_pressed(%_keyswitch[(%key[2] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1], %keyswitches_pressed[%key[2]])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[%key[2]], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %keyswitches_pressed[%key[2]])
    if(%keyswitches_pressed[%key[2]] = 1)
      $keyswitch_idx30 := %key[2]
      $color00 := %_keyswitch[(%key[2] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 10]
      call c_update__keycolor_mapped0
      %key[2] := $keyswitch_idx30
      %_keyswitch[(%key[2] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 10] := $color00
    end if
    if(%_keyswitch[(%key[2] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] = 127)
      %keyswitches_pressed[%key[2]] := 1
    end if
    if(%_keyswitch[%key[2] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 0)
      %keyswitches_pressed[%key[2]] := 0
    end if
    inc(%key[2])
  end while
  call color_keyswitches
  %key[3] := 0
  while(%key[3] <= 15) 
    select(%_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4])
      case 2
        %key[4] := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13]
        while(%key[4] <= %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14]) 
          $release_note00 := %key[4]
          $event_notes10 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          $note_id10 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          $release_id00 := $release_id
          $start_group10 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] + $title_groups
          $num_dynamic_layers40 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]
          $num_rr10 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
          call c_sustain_release0
          %key[4] := $release_note00
          %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $event_notes10
          %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $note_id10
          $release_id := $release_id00
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] := $num_dynamic_layers40
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr10
          inc(%key[4])
        end while
      case 3
        $note_held := 0
        %key[4] := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13]
        while(%key[4] <= %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14]) 
          $release_note20 := %key[4]
          $event_notes50 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          $note_id50 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          $release_id10 := $release_id
          $start_group40 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
          $num_dynamic_layers60 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]
          $num_rr40 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
          $trans_groups20 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 8]
          call c_legato_release0
          %key[4] := $release_note20
          %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $event_notes50
          %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $note_id50
          $release_id := $release_id10
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] := $start_group40
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] := $num_dynamic_layers60
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr40
          %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 8] := $trans_groups20
          inc(%key[4])
        end while
      case 0 to 1
        %key[4] := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13]
        while(%key[4] <= %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14]) 
          $release_note10 := %key[4]
          $event_notes30 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          $note_id30 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
          call c_one_shot_release0
          %key[4] := $release_note10
          %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $event_notes30
          %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $note_id30
          inc(%key[4])
        end while
    end select
    inc(%key[3])
  end while
end function
function analyze_vibrato_groups
  $lib__i := 0
  while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_groups) - 1)) 
    %vibrato_groups[$lib__i] := -1
    inc($lib__i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    select(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4])
      case 2
        $j := 0
        while($j <= (%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] - 1)) 
          %vibrato_groups[$ii] := %_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] + $j
          inc($ii)
          inc($j)
        end while
      case 3
        $j := 0
        while($j <= (((%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] + $title_groups) + %_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]) - 1)) 
          %vibrato_groups[$ii] := ((%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] + %_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]) + $title_groups) + $j
          inc($ii)
          inc($j)
        end while
    end select
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function c_analyze0
  if(%_keyswitch[$keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 1)
    call reset__keycolors
    $keys := 0
    while($keys <= 127) 
      $blip_note := play_note($keys, 1, 0, 1)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
      change_vol($blip_note, -2000000, 0)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3])
      wait(1)
      $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
      if($zone_id # -1)
        %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13] := $keys
        message("Low: " & !midi__note_names[$keys])
        $keys := 127
      end if
      fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
      inc($keys)
    end while
    $keys := 0
    while($keys <= 127) 
      $blip_note := play_note(127 - $keys, 1, 0, 1)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
      change_vol($blip_note, -2000000, 0)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3])
      wait(1)
      $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
      if($zone_id # -1)
        %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14] := 127 - $keys
        message("High: " & !midi__note_names[127 - $keys])
        $keys := 127
      end if
      fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
      inc($keys)
    end while
    $keys := 0
    while($keys <= 127) 
      %_keyswitch_mapped_notes[($keyswitch_idx00 * 128) + $keys] := 0
      $blip_note := play_note($keys, 1, 0, 1)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
      change_vol($blip_note, -2000000, 0)
      set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3])
      wait(1)
      $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
      if($zone_id # -1)
        message($zone_id & ", " & %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3])
        %_keyswitch_mapped_notes[($keyswitch_idx00 * 128) + $keys] := 1
      end if
      fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
      inc($keys)
    end while
    $keyswitch_idx30 := $keyswitch_idx00
    $color00 := %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 10]
    call c_update__keycolor_mapped0
    $keyswitch_idx00 := $keyswitch_idx30
    %_keyswitch[($keyswitch_idx00 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 10] := $color00
    call analyze_vibrato_groups
    call update__keyswitch
  end if
end function
function c_all_windows__show0
  $btn_home := $Boolean00
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean00])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean00])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  $btn_settings := $Boolean00
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean00])
  $btn_keyswitchSettings := $Boolean00
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_keyswitchSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean00])
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $Boolean00
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean00])
end function
function update__cc_dynamics
  set_controller(103, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_dynamics) - 0.) * 127.) / 1000000.) + 0.))
end function
function update__cc_expression
  set_controller(111, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_expression) - 0.) * 127.) / 1000000.) + 0.))
end function
function update__cc_vibrato
  set_controller(101, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_vibrato) - 0.) * 127.) / 1000000.) + 0.))
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, $sli_vibrato, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_EQ_GAIN_1"))
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, ($sli_vibrato * $current_pitchModulation) / 1000000, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function legato__init_arrays
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 1999) 
    if(%sus_release_time[$i] = 0)
      %sus_release_time[$i] := 280
    end if
    if(%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_fadeIn_time[$i] := 780000
    end if
    if(%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_fadeOut_time[$i] := 500000
    end if
    if(%trans_wait_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_wait_time[$i] := 696000
    end if
    if(%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] = 0)
      %sus_fadeIn_time[$i] := 780000
    end if
    if(%trans_zone_ids[$i] = 0)
      %trans_zone_ids[$i] := -1
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function c_one_shot0
  if($event_notes20 # $event_note10)
    $event_notes20 := $event_note10
    $rr_counter00 := ($rr_counter00 + 1) mod $num_rr20
    $note_id20 := play_note($event_note10, $event_velocity10, 0, $sample_duration00)
    set_event_par_arr($note_id20, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
    set_event_par_arr($note_id20, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $rr_counter00 + $start_group20)
  end if
end function
function update__vibrato
  $sli_vibIntensity := $sli_vibrato
  call update__cc_vibrato
end function
function update__vibIntensity
  $sli_vibrato := $sli_vibIntensity
  call update__cc_vibrato
end function

function update__pitchModulation

  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_pitchModulation) - 0.) * 200000.) / 1000000.) + 0.), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $current_pitchModulation := real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_pitchModulation) - 0.) * 200000.) / 1000000.) + 0.)
end function
function update__lfoFreq
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INTMOD_FREQUENCY, real_to_int((((int_to_real((($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]), 31) .or. sh_right($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note], 31)))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]), 31))) - 0.) * 200000.) / 1000000.) + 450000.), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__lfoRand
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lfoRandValues) - 1)) 
    %lfoRandValues[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%randNoteValues[$i]) - -500.) * (int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10) - - int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10))) / 1000.) + - int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__lfoFadeIn

    inc($i)
  end while
end function

function update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount = 0)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_presetName), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "EMPTY PRESET")
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_presetName), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !vibPresetNames[get_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
  end if
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 99) 
    if($i < $presetCount)
      set_menu_item_str(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, !vibPresetNames[$i])
      set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, 1)
    else
      set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, 0)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function load__array
  $i := 1
  while($i <= 99) 
    if(%uiControls[$i - 1] # 0)
      set_control_par(%uiControls[$i - 1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %vibrato_preset[$i])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0

function get__presetCount
  $presetCount := search(%vibPresetCount, 0)
  $presetCount := ($presetCount * (1 + (sh_right(100 - $presetCount, 31) .or. sh_right($presetCount, 31)))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - $presetCount, 31))
end function
function c_home__show0
  $btn_home := $Boolean30
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean30])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$Boolean30])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function
on ui_control($btn_activate0)
  %_keyswitch[0] := $btn_activate0
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))
    inc($i)
  end while
  call update__row_fonts
  call update__keyswitch
end on

on ui_control($mnu_keyswitch2)
  %_keyswitch[(2 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] := %keyswitches[$mnu_keyswitch2]
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])

    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]

  end while
  $ii := 0

      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if

    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])

on ui_control($btn_activate6)
  %_keyswitch[6 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] := $btn_activate6
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))
    inc($i)
  end while
  call update__row_fonts
  call update__keyswitch
end on

    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))
    inc($i)
  end while
  call color_keyswitches

    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))

on ui_control($mnu_keyswitch11)
  %_keyswitch[(11 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] := %keyswitches[$mnu_keyswitch11]
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])

  %_keyswitch[13 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] := $btn_activate13
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))
    inc($i)

on ui_control($btn_activate15)
  %_keyswitch[15 * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] := $btn_activate15
  $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 15) 
    $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN := $NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN + %_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%btn_keyswitches) - 1)) 
    if($NUM_KEYSWITCHES_SHOWN < 5)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 160)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 120)
      set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 13 + ((get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) + 8) * $ii))
    end if
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    set_control_par_str(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !keyswitch_names[$i])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 17)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !midi__note_names[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1]])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTPOS_Y, 38)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2)) - (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) / 2))
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, (get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + get_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT)) + 5)
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitches[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(%btn_keyswitches_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
    $ii := $ii + (%_keyswitch[$i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] .and. abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] - 127) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))

on ui_control($btn_keyswitches0)
  if(%keyswitches_purged[0] = 0)
    if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_keyswitches0), $CONTROL_PAR_KEY_ALT) = 0)
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 15) 
        %keyswitches_pressed[$i] := 0
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
    %keyswitches_pressed[0] := 1
    call update__keyswitch
  else
    $btn_keyswitches0 := 0
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_keyswitches_purge0)
  if($btn_keyswitches_purge0 = 1)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_keyswitches0), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_keyswitches0), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "btn_keyswitch")
  end if
  %keyswitches_purged[0] := $btn_keyswitches_purge0
  if(%keyswitches_pressed[0] = 1)
    %keyswitches_pressed[0] := 0
  end if
  call update__keyswitch
  $start_group := %_keyswitch[3]
  $num_dynamic_layers := %_keyswitch[5]
  $rr_count := %_keyswitch[6]
  $num_transitions := %_keyswitch[8]
  $sustain_fx := %_keyswitch[9]
  select(%_keyswitch[4])
    case 0 to 1
      %key[4] := $start_group
      while(%key[4] <= (($start_group + ($title_groups + $rr_count)) - 1)) 
        purge_group(%key[4], abs(sh_right(abs($btn_keyswitches_purge0) - 1, 31)))
        inc(%key[4])
      end while
    case 2
      %key[4] := $start_group
      while(%key[4] <= (($start_group + ((($title_groups + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers)) - 1)) 
        purge_group(%key[4], abs(sh_right(abs($btn_keyswitches_purge0) - 1, 31)))
        inc(%key[4])
      end while
    case 3
      %key[4] := $start_group
      while(%key[4] <= (($start_group + ((((((((((($title_groups + $rr_count) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + ($num_dynamic_layers * $sustain_fx)) + $title_groups) + $num_transitions) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers)) - 1)) 
        purge_group(%key[4], abs(sh_right(abs($btn_keyswitches_purge0) - 1, 31)))
        inc(%key[4])
      end while
  end select
end on

      while(%key[4] <= (($start_group + ((($title_groups + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers)) - 1)) 
        purge_group(%key[4], abs(sh_right(abs($btn_keyswitches_purge11) - 1, 31)))
        inc(%key[4])
      end while
    case 3
      %key[4] := $start_group
      while(%key[4] <= (($start_group + ((((((((((($title_groups + $rr_count) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers) + $title_groups) + ($num_dynamic_layers * $sustain_fx)) + $title_groups) + $num_transitions) + $title_groups) + $num_dynamic_layers)) - 1)) 
        purge_group(%key[4], abs(sh_right(abs($btn_keyswitches_purge11) - 1, 31)))
        inc(%key[4])
      end while
  end select
end on
