on persistence_changed
  if($pgs_init = 0)
    $pgs_init := 1
    call reset__keycolors
    call update__keyswitch
    call update__cc_dynamics
    call update__cc_expression
    call update__cc_vibrato
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 15) 
      if(%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4] = 3)
        wait_async(load_array_str(!trans_file_names, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_file_names.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(!intervals, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "intervals.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_zone_ids, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_zone_ids.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_zone_start, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_zone_start.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_event_volume, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_event_volume.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_wait_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_wait_time.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_fadeOut_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%sus_release_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "sus_release_time.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%sus_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%marked_samples, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "marked_samples.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(!sample_comments, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "sample_comments.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(!file_names_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "file_names_master.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%zone_ids_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "zone_ids_master.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%completed_elements, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[%_keyswitch[($i * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 11]] & "completed_elements.nka"))
        call legato__init_arrays
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    $i := 0
    while($i <= ($NUM_GROUPS - 1)) 
      set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, 1000000, $i, find_mod($i, "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"), find_target($i, find_mod($i, "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"), "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"))
      inc($i)
    end while
  end if
end on
on controller
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $sli_dynamics := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%CC[1]) - 0.) * 1000000.) / 127.) + 0.)
    call update__cc_dynamics
  end if
  if($CC_NUM = 111)
    $sli_expression := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%CC[111]) - 0.) * 1000000.) / 127.) + 0.)
    call update__cc_expression
  end if
  if($CC_NUM = 101)
    $sli_vibrato := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%CC[101]) - 0.) * 1000000.) / 127.) + 0.)
    $sli_vibIntensity := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%CC[101]) - 0.) * 1000000.) / 127.) + 0.)
    call update__cc_vibrato
  end if
  if($CC_NUM = 64)
    %key[3] := 0
    while(%key[3] <= 15) 
      if(%_keyswitch_mapped_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + $event_note] = 1)
        if(%keyswitches_pressed[%key[3]] = 1)
          select(%_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4])
            case 2
              if(%CC[64] = 0)
                %key[4] := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 13]
                while(%key[4] <= %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 14]) 
                  $release_note00 := %key[4]
                  $event_notes10 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
                  $note_id10 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]]
                  $release_id00 := $release_id
                  $start_group10 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] + $title_groups
                  $num_dynamic_layers40 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]
                  $num_rr10 := %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
                  call c_sustain_release0
                  %key[4] := $release_note00
                  %_keyswitch_event_notes[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $event_notes10
                  %_keyswitch_event_ids[(%key[3] * 128) + %key[4]] := $note_id10
                  $release_id := $release_id00
                  %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] := $num_dynamic_layers40
                  %_keyswitch[(%key[3] * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr10
                  inc(%key[4])
                end while
              end if
            case 3
          end select
        end if
      end if
      inc(%key[3])
    end while
  end if
end on
on note
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 1)
  ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
  $event_note := $EVENT_NOTE
  $event_velocity := $EVENT_VELOCITY
  message("Incoming Note: " & $EVENT_NOTE)
  if((search(%keyswitches, $EVENT_NOTE) # -1) and (%_keyswitch[search(%keyswitches, $event_note) * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 1))
    $key_it := 0
    while($key_it <= 15) 
      if((%_keyswitch[$key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 1) and (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] # 127))
        if(%KEY_DOWN[%keyswitches[$key_it]] # 1)
          %keyswitches_pressed[$key_it] := 0
        end if
      end if
      inc($key_it)
    end while
    %keyswitches_pressed[search(%keyswitches, $event_note)] := 1
    call update__keyswitch
  end if
  $key_it := 0
  while($key_it <= 15) 
    if(%_keyswitch_mapped_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] = 1)
      if(%keyswitches_pressed[$key_it] = 1)
        select(%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4])
          case 0
            message("one-shot")
            $event_note10 := $event_note
            $event_notes20 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $event_velocity10 := $event_velocity
            $note_id20 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $start_group20 := %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
            $num_rr20 := %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
            $rr_counter00 := %_keyswitch_rr_counter[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $sample_duration00 := 0
            call c_one_shot0
            $event_note := $event_note10
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $event_notes20
            $event_velocity := $event_velocity10
            %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $note_id20
            %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] := $start_group20
            %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr20
            %_keyswitch_rr_counter[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $rr_counter00
          case 1
            message("adhsr")
            $event_note10 := $event_note
            $event_notes20 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $event_velocity10 := $event_velocity
            $note_id20 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $start_group20 := %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
            $num_rr20 := %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
            $rr_counter00 := %_keyswitch_rr_counter[($key_it * 128) + $event_note]
            $sample_duration00 := -1
            call c_one_shot0
            $event_note := $event_note10
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $event_notes20
            $event_velocity := $event_velocity10
            %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $note_id20
            %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] := $start_group20
            %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr20
            %_keyswitch_rr_counter[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $rr_counter00
          case 2
            message("sustain")
            if(%_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] = -1)
              %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $event_note
              %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := play_note($event_note, $event_velocity, 0, 0)
              set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
              $dyn := 0
              while($dyn <= (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] - 1)) 
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $dyn + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3])
                inc($dyn)
              end while
            end if
          case 3
            $atk_group := %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
            $atk_sus_group := ($atk_group + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]) + $title_groups
            $sus_group := ($atk_sus_group + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]) + $title_groups
            $sus_fx_group := ($sus_group + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]) + $title_groups
            $trans_group := ($sus_fx_group + (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] * %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 9])) + $title_groups
            $num_notes := 0
            message(%keyswitches[15] + 1)
            $i := %keyswitches[15] + 1
            while($i <= (num_elements(%KEY_DOWN) - 1)) 
              $num_notes := %KEY_DOWN[$i] + $num_notes
              inc($i)
            end while
            message("num_notes: " & $num_notes)
            $interval := $EVENT_NOTE - $last_note
            if((($num_notes > 1) and ($event_note # $last_note)) and ($is_attack # -1))
              $is_attack := 0
              if(abs($interval) <= 12)
                $blip_note := play_note(($event_note * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right($interval, 31) + 1) - 1, 31))) + ($last_note * (sh_right($interval, 31) + 1)), (abs($interval) * 5) + ((sh_right($interval, 31) + 1) * 60), 0, -1)
                change_vol($blip_note, -200000, 0)
                set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $trans_group + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 12])
                wait(1)
                if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
                  $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, -1)
                else
                  $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
                end if
                fade_out(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $last_note], %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] * 1000, 1)
                %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $last_note] := -1
                fade_out($last_transition, 240000, 1)
                fade_out($blip_note, 1, 1)
                $transition_id := play_note(($event_note * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right($interval, 31) + 1) - 1, 31))) + ($last_note * (sh_right($interval, 31) + 1)), (abs($interval) * 5) + ((sh_right($interval, 31) + 1) * 60), real_to_int((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) / 48000.) * 1000000.), 0)
                set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx], 3)
                set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_fadeOut_time[$trans_idx], 5)
                set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $trans_group + %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 12])
                change_vol($transition_id, %trans_event_volume[$trans_idx], 0)
                %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := play_note($event_note, 69, $sus_s_start, -1)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx], 0)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx], 2)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                $i := 0
                while($i <= (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_group)
                  inc($i)
                end while
                $i := 0
                while($i <= ((%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] * %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 9]) - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_fx_group)
                  inc($i)
                end while
              else
                fade_out(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $last_note], 152000, 1)
                %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $last_note] := -1
                %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := play_note($event_note, $EVENT_VELOCITY, $sus_s_start, -1)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, 150000, 0)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, 780000, 2)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                $i := 0
                while($i <= (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_group)
                  inc($i)
                end while
                $i := 0
                while($i <= ((%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] * %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 9]) - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_fx_group)
                  inc($i)
                end while
              end if
            else
              if($num_notes = 1)
                message("Initial Note")
                $last_note := $event_note
                set_event_par_arr($ALL_EVENTS, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                $is_attack := abs(sh_right(abs($NOTE_HELD) - 1, 31))
                %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := play_note($event_note, 69, 250000, -1)
                $attack_id := play_note($event_note, ((($EVENT_VELOCITY * (1 + (sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31) .or. sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31)))) - ((%CC[103] - 20) * sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31))) - ((%CC[103] + 20) * sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31))) - ((((($EVENT_VELOCITY * (1 + (sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31) .or. sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31)))) - ((%CC[103] - 20) * sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31))) - ((%CC[103] + 20) * sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31))) - 127) .and. sh_right(127 - ((($EVENT_VELOCITY * (1 + (sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31) .or. sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31)))) - ((%CC[103] - 20) * sh_right($EVENT_VELOCITY - (%CC[103] - 20), 31))) - ((%CC[103] + 20) * sh_right((%CC[103] + 20) - $EVENT_VELOCITY, 31))), 31)), 0, 0)
                set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
                %key[5] := 0
                while(%key[5] <= (%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, %key[5] + $atk_sus_group)
                  inc(%key[5])
                end while
                %key[5] := 0
                while(%key[5] <= ((%_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] * %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 9]) - 1)) 
                  set_event_par_arr(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note], $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, %key[5] + $sus_fx_group)
                  inc(%key[5])
                end while
                set_event_par_arr($attack_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $atk_group + %rr_counter[$event_note])
                %rr_counter[$event_note] := (%rr_counter[$event_note] + 1) mod %_keyswitch[($key_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
              else
                note_off(%_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_it * 128) + $event_note])
              end if
            end if
            $last_transition := $transition_id
            $last_note := $event_note
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_it * 128) + $event_note] := $event_note
        end select
      end if
    end if
    inc($key_it)
  end while
end on
on release
  $release_note := $EVENT_NOTE
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 0)
  if(search(%keyswitches, $EVENT_NOTE) # -1)
    if((%_keyswitch[search(%keyswitches, $release_note) * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)] = 1) and (%_keyswitch[(search(%keyswitches, $release_note) * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 1] # 127))
      set_key_pressed($release_note, 1)
    end if
  end if
  $key_rel_it := 0
  while($key_rel_it <= 15) 
    if(%_keyswitch_mapped_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] = 1)
      if(%keyswitches_pressed[$key_rel_it] = 1)
        select(%_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 4])
          case 0
            $release_note10 := $release_note
            $event_notes30 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            $note_id30 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            call c_one_shot_release0
            $release_note := $release_note10
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $event_notes30
            %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $note_id30
          case 1
            $release_note10 := $release_note
            $event_notes30 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            $note_id30 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            call c_one_shot_release0
            $release_note := $release_note10
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $event_notes30
            %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $note_id30
          case 2
            if(%CC[64] = 0)
              $release_note00 := $release_note
              $event_notes10 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
              $note_id10 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
              $release_id00 := $release_id
              $start_group10 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
              $num_dynamic_layers40 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]
              $num_rr10 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
              call c_sustain_release0
              $release_note := $release_note00
              %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $event_notes10
              %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $note_id10
              $release_id := $release_id00
              %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] := $start_group10
              %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] := $num_dynamic_layers40
              %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr10
            end if
          case 3
            $note_held := %KEY_DOWN[$event_note]
            $release_note20 := $release_note
            $event_notes50 := %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            $note_id50 := %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note]
            $release_id10 := $release_id
            $start_group40 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3]
            $num_dynamic_layers60 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5]
            $num_rr40 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6]
            $trans_groups20 := %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 8]
            call c_legato_release0
            $release_note := $release_note20
            %_keyswitch_event_notes[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $event_notes50
            %_keyswitch_event_ids[($key_rel_it * 128) + $release_note] := $note_id50
            $release_id := $release_id10
            %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 3] := $start_group40
            %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 5] := $num_dynamic_layers60
            %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 6] := $num_rr40
            %_keyswitch[($key_rel_it * num_elements(%keyswitch_idx)) + 8] := $trans_groups20
        end select
      end if
    end if
    inc($key_rel_it)
  end while
end on
on ui_control($btn_vibratoSettings)
  $Boolean00 := 0
  call c_all_windows__show0
  $btn_vibratoSettings := 1
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $btn_vibratoSettings
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_vibratoSettings])
end on
on ui_control($sli_vibrato)
  call update__vibrato
end on
on ui_control($sli_vibIntensity)
  call update__vibIntensity
end on
on ui_control($sli_envRateCurve)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], $sli_envRateCurve, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_rate__hold := ($sli_envRateHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_rate__sustain := ($sli_envRateSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[0])
  $last_time_envRateCurve := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateCurve) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envRateCurve, !envRateNames[0])
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_envRateAttack)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], $sli_envRateAttack, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_rate__hold := ($sli_envRateHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_rate__sustain := ($sli_envRateSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateAttack), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[1])
  $last_time_envRateAttack := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateAttack) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envRateAttack, !envRateNames[1])
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_envRateHold)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], $sli_envRateHold, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_rate__hold := ($sli_envRateHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envRateDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_rate__sustain := ($sli_envRateSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateHold), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[2])
  $last_time_envRateHold := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateHold) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envRateHold, !envRateNames[2])
  end if
end on

    end if

  end while

    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while

    end if

  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[4])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envRateSustain / 10000) & " %")
  $last_time_envRateSustain := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateSustain) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envRateSustain, !envRateNames[4])
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_rateEnv)
  call update__rateEnv
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_rateEnv), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real($sli_rateEnv / 1000) / 10.) & " %")
  $last_time_rateEnv := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_rateEnv) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_rateEnv, "Rate Envelope")
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_envIntCurve)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], $sli_envIntCurve, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_int__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_int__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_int__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_int__hold := ($sli_envIntHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_int__sustain := ($sli_envIntSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[0])
  $last_time_envIntCurve := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envIntCurve) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envIntCurve, !envRateNames[0])
  end if
end on

    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntDecay), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[3], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[3])
  $last_time_envIntDecay := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envIntDecay) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envIntDecay, !envRateNames[3])
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_envIntSustain)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], $sli_envIntSustain, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10., (log(1.5) / log(10.)) + (0.51 * ((log(0.056) / log(10.)) - (log(1.5) / log(10.)))))
  $tbl_int__release_idx := 93
  ~tbl_int__attack := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntAttack) - 0.) * (~tbl_int__attack_point - 1.5)) / 1000000.) + 1.5
  $tbl_int__hold := ($sli_envIntHold * 18) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__decay := (((int_to_real($sli_envIntDecay) - 0.) * 14200.) / 1000000.) + 800.
  $tbl_int__sustain := ($sli_envIntSustain * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__release := 30200.
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 10.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.) * 200.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1. / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 4.99) / 14200.) + 0.01))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.) * 300.) / 14200.) + 0.))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.) * 1000.) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.)) + 0.)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i, 31)))) - (125 * sh_right(125 - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real(($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * -1.) / 500000.) + 1.)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.) * 1.) / 500000.) + 0.))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := (%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx])) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 124) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31)))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) * 880) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[4])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envIntSustain / 10000) & " %")
  $last_time_envIntSustain := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envIntSustain) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_envIntSustain, !envRateNames[4])
  end if
end on

  call update__intEnv
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_intEnv), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real($sli_intEnv / 1000) / 10.) & " %")

on ui_control($btn_prevPreset)
  $btn_prevPreset := 0
  $mnu_preset := (($mnu_preset - 1) + $presetCount) mod $presetCount
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
    message("load preset: " & ", " & @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_nextPreset)
  $btn_nextPreset := 0
  $mnu_preset := ($mnu_preset + 1) mod $presetCount
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
    message("load preset: " & ", " & @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_savePreset)
  $btn_savePreset := 0
  $load_id := load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka")
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka"))
  if($load_id # -1)
    %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
    !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := @txt_presetName
    save_array(!vibPresetNames, 1)
    save_array(%vibPresetCount, 1)
    $mnu_preset := $presetCount
    $presetCount := (($presetCount + 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - ($presetCount + 1), 31) .or. sh_right($presetCount + 1, 31)))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - ($presetCount + 1), 31))
    $preset_scan := 1
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
  end if
  %vibrato_preset[0] := 0
  $i := 1
  while($i <= 99) 
    if(%uiControls[$i - 1] # 0)
      %vibrato_preset[$i] := get_control_par(%uiControls[$i - 1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka")
  call update__preset__menu
end on
on ui_control($btn_deletePreset)
  $btn_deletePreset := 0
  %vibrato_preset[0] := 1
  save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
    if($i # $mnu_preset)
      !vibPresetNames[$ii] := !vibPresetNames[$i]
      %vibPresetCount[$ii] := %vibPresetCount[$i]
      inc($ii)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  save_array(!vibPresetNames, 1)
  save_array(%vibPresetCount, 1)
  $presetCount := (($presetCount - 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - ($presetCount - 1), 31) .or. sh_right($presetCount - 1, 31)))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - ($presetCount - 1), 31))
  $mnu_preset := (($mnu_preset - 1) * (1 + (sh_right($presetCount - ($mnu_preset - 1), 31) .or. sh_right($mnu_preset - 1, 31)))) - ($presetCount * sh_right($presetCount - ($mnu_preset - 1), 31))
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
    message("load preset: " & ", " & @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mouse_nka)
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DROP)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, !NI_DND_ITEMS_ARRAY[0]))
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_scanPresets)
  if($preset_scan = 0)
    $preset_scan := 1
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
      %vibPresetCount[$i] := 0
      !vibPresetNames[$i] := ""
      inc($i)
    end while
    $lib__i := 0
    while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset2) - 1)) 
      %vibrato_preset2[$lib__i] := 0
      inc($lib__i)
    end while
    $lib__i := 0
    while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
      %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
      inc($lib__i)
    end while
    $presetCount := 0
    fs_navigate(get_ui_id($file_browser), 1)
  end if
end on
on ui_control($file_browser)
  message("File Browser triggered")
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 2)))
  if(($preset_scan = 1) and (%vibrato_preset[0] # -420))
    if(%vibrato_preset[0] = 0)
      if(not array_equal(%vibrato_preset, %vibrato_preset2))
        !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 0)
        %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
        inc($presetCount)
      end if
      $lib__i := 0
      while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
        %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
        inc($lib__i)
      end while
    else
      if(((%vibrato_preset[0] = 0) or (%vibrato_preset[0] = 1)) and (get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_KEY_ALT) = 1))
        message("Scanning for deleted")
        if(not array_equal(%vibrato_preset, %vibrato_preset2))
          !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 0)
          %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
          inc($presetCount)
          %vibrato_preset[0] := 0
          save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 2))
        end if
        $lib__i := 0
        while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
          %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
          inc($lib__i)
        end while
      end if
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    fs_navigate(get_ui_id($file_browser), 1)
  else
    message("The end")
    save_array(!vibPresetNames, 1)
    save_array(%vibPresetCount, 1)
    call get__presetCount
    $preset_scan := 0
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    call update__preset__menu
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
    message("load preset: " & ", " & @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mnu_preset)
  call update__preset__menu
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
  message("load preset: " & ", " & @vibrato_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
  call load__array
end on
on async_complete
  if($NI_ASYNC_ID = $save_id)
    if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = 1)
      $save_id := -1
    else
      if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = 0)
        $save_id := 0
      end if
    end if
  end if
  if($NI_ASYNC_ID = $load_id)
    if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = 1)
      $load_id := -1
    else
      if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = 0)
        $load_id := 0
      end if
    end if
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_home)
  $Boolean00 := 0
  call c_all_windows__show0
  $btn_home := 1
  $Boolean30 := $btn_home
  call c_home__show0
  $btn_home := $Boolean30
end on
on ui_control($sli_dynamics)
  set_controller(103, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_dynamics) - 0.) * 127.) / 1000000.) + 0.))
end on
on ui_control($sli_expression)
  set_controller(111, real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_expression) - 0.) * 127.) / 1000000.) + 0.))
end on
on ui_control($btn_reverb)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_BYPASS, abs($btn_reverb - 1), -1, 1, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
end on
on ui_control($mnu_revtype)
  %async_ids[0] := load_ir_sample(!revtypes[$mnu_revtype], 1, 1)
  wait_async(%async_ids[0])
end on
on ui_control($btn_next_rev)
  $btn_next_rev := 0
  $mnu_revtype := ($mnu_revtype + 1) mod num_elements(!revtypes)
  %async_ids[0] := load_ir_sample(!revtypes[$mnu_revtype], 1, 1)
  wait_async(%async_ids[0])
end on
on ui_control($btn_prev_rev)
  $btn_prev_rev := 0
  $mnu_revtype := (($mnu_revtype - 1) + num_elements(!revtypes)) mod num_elements(!revtypes)
  %async_ids[0] := load_ir_sample(!revtypes[$mnu_revtype], 1, 1)
  wait_async(%async_ids[0])
end on
on ui_control($sli_reverbmix)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_DRY_LEVEL, %drywet[(1000000 - $sli_reverbmix) / 1000], -1, 1, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %drywet[$sli_reverbmix / 1000], -1, 1, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_reverbmix), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_reverbmix / 10000) & " %")
  $last_time_reverbmix := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_reverbmix) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_reverbmix, "Mix")
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_eq)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_BYPASS, abs($btn_eq - 1), -1, 0, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
end on
on ui_control($sli_lowGain)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_GAIN, $sli_lowGain, -1, 0, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_lowGain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_GAIN, -1, 0, $NI_INSERT_BUS) & " dB")
  $last_time_lowGain := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_lowGain) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_lowGain, "Low")
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_highGain)
  set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN, $sli_highGain, -1, 0, $NI_INSERT_BUS)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_highGain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN, -1, 0, $NI_INSERT_BUS) & " dB")
  $last_time_highGain := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_highGain) > 795)
    set_text($lbl_highGain, "High")
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mnu_dynamic_cc)
  $num_dynamic_cc := get_menu_item_value(get_ui_id($mnu_dynamic_cc), get_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_dynamic_cc), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE))
  call update__cc_dynamics
end on
on ui_control($btn_settings)
  if($btn_settings = 1)
    $Boolean00 := 0
    call c_all_windows__show0
    $btn_settings := 1
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[1])
  else
    $Boolean00 := 0
    call c_all_windows__show0
    $Boolean30 := 1
    call c_home__show0
  end if
end on
